				<article id="post-3409" class="post-3409 page type-page status-publish hentry">

				
					<div class="entry-content">
					<div class="et-l et-l--post">
			<div class="et_builder_inner_content et_pb_gutters3"><div class="et_pb_section et_pb_section_0 et_section_regular" >
				
				
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_row et_pb_row_0">
				<div class="et_pb_column et_pb_column_4_4 et_pb_column_0  et_pb_css_mix_blend_mode_passthrough et-last-child">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_0  et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><p>*Information below may be subject to change* Samueli Engineering policies are different from the College of Letters and Science &#8211; therefore, you should check with your <a href="https://www.seasoasa.ucla.edu/counselors">OASA counselor</a>, through Message Center or by scheduling an appointment, whenever you have a question.</p>
<p><h3 style="border-bottom: 1px solid;">Popular FAQs</h3>
<dl>
</p>
<dt class="show_hide" style="cursor: pointer; font-weight:normal;"><span class="toggle-plus">+</span> Counselors Availability: When are the academic counselors available?</dt>
<dd style="display:none">
<blockquote><p><p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; outline: 0px; border: 0px currentColor; border-image: none; color: rgb(34, 34, 34); line-height: 23.8px; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;">UPDATE: Please refer to&nbsp;our&nbsp;<a style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 11px;" href="https://www.seasoasa.ucla.edu/" data-mce-href="https://www.seasoasa.ucla.edu/" data-mce-style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 11px;">home page</a>&nbsp;to schedule an appointment and for updated virtual walk-in times.&nbsp;<br><br>The Counselors and Staff of the UCLA Samueli School of Engineering&nbsp;Office of Academic and Student Affairs (OASA), 6426 BH, are available to assist you and answer your questions. You can send a message through message center to your <a href="http://www.seasoasa.ucla.edu/counselors/" data-mce-href="http://www.seasoasa.ucla.edu/counselors/">OASA Counselor</a>, call (310)825-9580, or go to MyUCLA to schedule an appointment. We do not do same day appointments.</p><p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; outline: 0px; border: 0px currentColor; border-image: none; color: rgb(34, 34, 34); line-height: 23.8px; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;">&nbsp;</p><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 23px 16px; outline: 0px; border: 0px currentColor; border-image: none; color: rgb(34, 34, 34); line-height: 26px; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 23px 16px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 26px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;"><li style="background: none; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; border: 0px currentColor; border-image: none; vertical-align: baseline;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;"><strong style="background: none; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; border: 0px currentColor; border-image: none; vertical-align: baseline;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;">Advising by Appointment</strong><ul style="background: none; margin: 0px; padding: 2px 0px 2px 20px; outline: 0px; border: 0px currentColor; border-image: none; vertical-align: baseline;" type="disc" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 2px 0px 2px 20px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; list-style: disc; background: transparent;"><li style="background: none; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; border: 0px currentColor; border-image: none; vertical-align: baseline;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;">Available Mondays, Tuesdays, Wednesday afternoons and Fridays.</li><li style="background: none; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; border: 0px currentColor; border-image: none; vertical-align: baseline;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;">We do not do same day appointments.</li><li style="background: none; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; border: 0px currentColor; border-image: none; vertical-align: baseline;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;">Go to <a href="https://be.my.ucla.edu/apps/Appointments/SelfService/Search" data-mce-href="https://be.my.ucla.edu/apps/Appointments/SelfService/Search">MyUCLA</a> or Call (310) 825-9580 to set up an appointment.</li></ul></li><li style="background: none; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; border: 0px currentColor; border-image: none; vertical-align: baseline;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;"><strong style="background: none; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; border: 0px currentColor; border-image: none; vertical-align: baseline;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;">&nbsp; Walk-in Counseling</strong><ul style="background: none; margin: 0px; padding: 2px 0px 2px 20px; outline: 0px; border: 0px currentColor; border-image: none; vertical-align: baseline;" type="disc" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 2px 0px 2px 20px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; list-style: disc; background: transparent;"><li style="background: none; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; border: 0px currentColor; border-image: none; vertical-align: baseline;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;">&nbsp;Available Tuesdays (9:00am-11:00am), Wednesdays (10:00am-12:00pm) and Thursdays (2:00pm-4:00pm)</li><li style="background: none; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; border: 0px currentColor; border-image: none; vertical-align: baseline;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;">&nbsp;On a first-come limited basis (normally 15 minute appointments.)</li><li style="background: none; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; border: 0px currentColor; border-image: none; vertical-align: baseline;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;">&nbsp;During peak advising periods, students should be prepared to have a significant wait period to see a counselor depending on the number of students who are signed in ahead on the walk-in advising check-in list and especially if you are requesting to see a specific counselor. Plan accordingly and give yourself a sufficient amount of time.&nbsp; Limited to UCLA Samueli School of Engineering students only.&nbsp; If you are a non-UCLA Samueli School of Engineering student and are considering a change of major to&nbsp;UCLA Engineering, please sign up for our&nbsp;<a style="background: none; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; border: 0px currentColor; border-image: none; color: rgb(30, 75, 135); text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline;" title="Change of Majors" href="http://www.seasoasa.ucla.edu/change-of-major/" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration: none; color: #1e4b87; background: transparent;" data-mce-href="http://www.seasoasa.ucla.edu/change-of-major/">change of major workshop</a>.<br><br><!-- [if gte mso 9]><xml>

<dt class="show_hide" style="cursor: pointer; font-weight:normal;"><span class="toggle-plus">+</span> Deadlines to drop/add: When are the deadlines to drop/add a course?</dt>
<dd style="display:none">
<blockquote><p><p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;">The deadline to:</p><blockquote style="margin: 20px 0px 30px; padding: 10px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; quotes: none; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; line-height: 23.8px; border: 1px solid #2ea3f2 !important; background: #f8f8f8;" data-mce-style="margin: 20px 0px 30px; padding: 10px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; quotes: none; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; line-height: 23.8px; border: 1px solid #2ea3f2 !important; background: #f8f8f8;"><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 23px 16px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 26px; background: transparent;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 23px 16px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 26px; background: transparent;" type="disc"><li style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;"><strong style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;">Drop</strong>&nbsp;an&nbsp;<strong style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;"><em style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;">Impacted</em></strong>&nbsp;course is the last business day (usually Friday) of&nbsp;<strong style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;">2<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; height: 0px; line-height: 1; position: relative; bottom: 0.8em; background: transparent;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; height: 0px; line-height: 1; position: relative; bottom: 0.8em; background: transparent;">nd&nbsp;</span></strong>Week at&nbsp;<strong style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;">5 PM</strong>.</li><li style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;"><strong style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;">Add</strong>&nbsp;a course is the last business day of&nbsp;<strong style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;">3<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; height: 0px; line-height: 1; position: relative; bottom: 0.8em; background: transparent;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; height: 0px; line-height: 1; position: relative; bottom: 0.8em; background: transparent;">rd</span></strong>&nbsp;Week at&nbsp;<strong style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;">5 PM</strong>.</li><li style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;"><strong style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;">4<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;">5 PM</strong>.</li><li style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;">Change</strong>&nbsp;a course to&nbsp;<strong style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;">P/NP&nbsp;</strong>is the last business day of&nbsp;<strong style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;">6<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;">5 PM</strong>.</li></ul></blockquote><p style="margin: 0px; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; <dt class="show_hide" style="cursor: pointer; font-weight:normal;"><span class="toggle-plus">+</span> Academic Probation: What does it mean if I’m on academic probation or subject to dismissal?</dt>
<dd style="display:none">
<blockquote><p><span style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;" data-mce-style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;">You will be placed on probation if your term or overall grade-point average (GPA) falls between 1.5 and 1.99. You will be subject to&nbsp;</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;" data-mce-style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;">dismissal if your grade-point average in any one term is less than 1.5 OR if you do not earn at least a C (2.0) average in any one term when you were on probation OR if you do not end probation by the end of the next term. Subject to Dismissal does not mean that you are going to be immediately dismissed; however, you must make an appointment to meet with your OASA Counselor who will explain the conditions under which you will be allowed to continue. You should meet with your Counselor in the Office of Academic and Student Affairs (OASA, 6426 BH) if you have been notified that you are on academic probation or subject to dismissal.</span></p></blockquote>
</dd>
<p></p>
<dt class="show_hide" style="cursor: pointer; font-weight:normal;"><span class="toggle-plus">+</span> Academic Standing: What does it mean if I’m in “good academic standing”?</dt>
<dd style="display:none">
<blockquote><p><span style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;" data-mce-style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;">You are in “good academic standing” if at the close of a regular term you have attained a “C” (2.0) average for the term and a cumulative “C” (2.0) average in all University work.</span></p></blockquote>
</dd>
<p></p>

For UCLA Samueli School of Engineering, if you graduated summa cum laude, you’re in the top 5% of your class; magna cum laude, top 10%; cum laude, top 20%.”</p><p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; <dt class="show_hide" style="cursor: pointer; font-weight:normal;"><span class="toggle-plus">+</span> Counselors Availability: When are the academic counselors available?</dt>
<dd style="display:none">
<blockquote><p><p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; outline: 0px; border: 0px currentColor; border-image: none; color: rgb(34, 34, 34); line-height: 23.8px; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;">UPDATE: Please refer to&nbsp;our&nbsp;<a style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 11px;" href="https://www.seasoasa.ucla.edu/" data-mce-href="https://www.seasoasa.ucla.edu/" data-mce-style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 11px;">home page</a>&nbsp;to schedule an appointment and for updated virtual walk-in times.&nbsp;<br><br>The Counselors and Staff of the UCLA Samueli School of Engineering&nbsp;Office of Academic and Student Affairs (OASA), 6426 BH, are available to assist you and answer your questions. You can send a message through message center to your <a href="http://www.seasoasa.ucla.edu/counselors/" data-mce-href="http://www.seasoasa.ucla.edu/counselors/">OASA Counselor</a>, call (310)825-9580, or go to MyUCLA to schedule an appointment. We do not do same day appointments.</p><p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; outline: 0px; border: 0px currentColor; border-image: none; color: rgb(34, 34, 34); line-height: 23.8px; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 23px 16px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 26px; color: #222222; vertical-align: baseline;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;">Available Mondays, Tuesdays, Wednesday afternoons and Fridays.</li><li style="background: none; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; border: 0px currentColor; border-image: none; vertical-align: baseline;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;">We do not do same day appointments.</li><li style="background: none; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; border: 0px currentColor; border-image: none; vertical-align: baseline;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;">Go to <a href="https://be.my.ucla.edu/apps/Appointments/SelfService/Search" data-mce-href="https://be.my.ucla.edu/apps/Appointments/SelfService/Search">MyUCLA</a> or Call (310) 825-9580 to set up an appointment.</li></ul></li><li style="background: none; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; border: 0px currentColor; border-image: none; vertical-align: baseline;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;"><strong style="background: none; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; border: 0px currentColor; border-image: none; vertical-align: baseline;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; border: 0px currentColor; border-image: none; vertical-align: baseline;" type="disc" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 2px 0px 2px 20px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; list-style: disc; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;">&nbsp;Available Tuesdays (9:00am-11:00am), Wednesdays (10:00am-12:00pm) and Thursdays (2:00pm-4:00pm)</li><li style="background: none; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; border: 0px currentColor; border-image: none; vertical-align: baseline;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;">&nbsp;On a first-come limited basis (normally 15 minute appointments.)</li><li style="background: none; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; border: 0px currentColor; border-image: none; vertical-align: baseline;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;">&nbsp;During peak advising periods, students should be prepared to have a significant wait period to see a counselor depending on the number of students who are signed in ahead on the walk-in advising check-in list and especially if you are requesting to see a specific counselor. <dt class="show_hide" style="cursor: pointer; font-weight:normal;"><span class="toggle-plus">+</span> Holds: How can I remove a hold on my record?</dt>
<dd style="display:none">
<blockquote><p><span style="color: #222222; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: small;" data-mce-style="color: #222222; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: small;">Only the department that placed that&nbsp;</span><span class="il" style="color: #222222; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: small;" data-mce-style="color: #222222; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: small;">hold</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: small;" data-mce-style="color: #222222; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: small;">&nbsp;can remove it for you. You should contact the department who placed the&nbsp;</span><span class="il" style="color: #222222; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: small;" data-mce-style="color: #222222; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: small;">hold</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: small;" data-mce-style="color: #222222; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: small;">&nbsp;and they will tell you what you must do to have the&nbsp;</span><span class="il" style="color: #222222; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: small;" data-mce-style="color: #222222; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: small;">hold</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: small;" data-mce-style="color: #222222; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: small;">&nbsp;removed. Usually there will be a number or email you can contact next to the&nbsp;</span><span class="il" style="color: #222222; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: small;" data-mce-style="color: #222222; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: small;">hold</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: small;" data-mce-style="color: #222222; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: small;">.</span></p></blockquote>
</dd>
<p></p>
<dt class="show_hide" style="cursor: pointer; font-weight:normal;"><span class="toggle-plus">+</span> Incomplete Grade: What is an “I” Incomplete grade?</dt>
<dd style="display:none">
<blockquote><p><p>Incomplete Grades</p><p>The instructor may assign the incomplete (I) grade under the following conditions: the student must ask the Instructor for the I grade, the student’s work must be of passing quality and the reasons for requesting the I grade must be of sufficient gravity to warrant an incomplete grade (such as illness or other serious problem). It is the student’s responsibility to discuss with the instructor the possibility of receiving an I grade as opposed to a nonpassing grade. &nbsp;However, a professor may certainly reach out to a student and suggest an incomplete if they feel the situation is appropriate.</p><p>How&nbsp;do these rules apply to students&nbsp;who miss a final exam? &nbsp;If a student does not take the final exam and never contacts the instructor, the student receives the grade they have earned with their completed work up to that point, usually an F.&nbsp; Consistent with the above discussion, if a student contacts the instructor providing a&nbsp;&nbsp; valid and documented reason (e.g. illness), the student will receive an incomplete (I), if and only if the student has a passing grade (C- or higher) at that point.&nbsp; Again, a professor may reach out to a student who misses a final if they feel it is appropriate.&nbsp; If an incomplete is given, the student must make arrangements with the instructor to take the final exam the following quarter. &nbsp;</p><p class="MsoNormal">&nbsp;</p>If an I grade is assigned, students may receive unit credit and grade points by satisfactorily completing the coursework as specified by the instructor. Students should not re-enroll in the course; if they do, it is recorded twice on the transcript. If the work is not completed by the end of the next full term in residence, the I grade lapses to an F, NP, or U as appropriate. The College or school may extend the deadline in unusual cases (not applicable to graduate students). Once an Incomplete (I) grade is assigned, it remains on the transcript along with the passing grade students may later receive for the course.</p></blockquote>
</dd>
<p></p>
<dt class="show_hide" style="cursor: pointer; font-weight:normal;"><span class="toggle-plus">+</span> Pass/No Pass: Is it possible to take a course on P/NP grading?</dt>
<dd style="display:none">
<blockquote><p><h2 style="box-sizing: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 10px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 21px; text-size-adjust: 100%; vertical-align: baseline; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; color: rgb(43, 43, 43); line-height: 1em; font-weight: 500; font-family: Lato, Helvetica, Arial, Lucida, sans-serif;">Passed/Not Passed (P/NP) Eligibility</h2><p style="box-sizing: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; text-size-adjust: 100%; vertical-align: baseline; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; line-height: 1.6em; color: rgb(43, 43, 43); font-family: Lato, Helvetica, Arial, Lucida, sans-serif;">Required courses (e.g. math, science, prep for the major, major courses, major electives, technical breadth, Engl Comp 3, ethics, etc.)&nbsp; for all UCLA Samueli School of Engineering majors and minors must be taken for a letter grade (unless the course is graded P/NP only)<span style="box-sizing: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; text-size-adjust: 100%; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;">.<br style="box-sizing: inherit;"></span>If an engineering course is LG this means students do not have the PNP option regardless of major.<br style="box-sizing: inherit;">For engineering students, ONLY courses that are PNP ONLY or General Education (GE) or excess units (not required courses) AND<br style="box-sizing: inherit;">also have the Student&nbsp; Option (SO) grade designation (Listed in the Schedule of Classes as may be taken for Letter grade or Pass/Not Pass) may be taken for P/NP if the student is in good academic standing.</p><p style="box-sizing: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; text-size-adjust: 100%; vertical-align: baseline; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; line-height: 1.6em; color: rgb(43, 43, 43); font-family: Lato, Helvetica, Arial, Lucida, sans-serif;">In addition to the above, further restrictions on taking a course P.NP are:</p><p style="box-sizing: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; text-size-adjust: 100%; vertical-align: baseline; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; line-height: 1.6em; color: rgb(43, 43, 43); font-family: Lato, Helvetica, Arial, Lucida, sans-serif;">A) an engineering student can enroll in courses that are P/NP grading&nbsp; only up to four units in one quarter without any additional UCLA Samueli School of Engineering restrictions or requirements.&nbsp; A student who has not elected the P/NP option, if eligible, in the immediate previous term (last regular term enrolled (excludes summer)&nbsp;<a href="https://www.seasoasa.ucla.edu/petition-process/" style="box-sizing: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; text-size-adjust: 100%; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent; color: rgb(13, 68, 129);">may petition</a>&nbsp;to take two grading optional courses (maximum 10 units) P/NP.<br style="box-sizing: inherit;">B) For courses that are grading optional (letter grade OR P/NP), students are allowed to enroll in one grading option course (up to 5 units) under P/NP in a quarter if they are:</p><ul style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; text-size-adjust: 100%; vertical-align: baseline; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; line-height: 26px; color: rgb(43, 43, 43); font-family: Lato, Helvetica, Arial, Lucida, sans-serif;"><li style="box-sizing: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; text-size-adjust: 100%; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent; list-style-type: disc;">are in good academic standing (2.0 or higher term and cumulative GPA) and</li><li style="box-sizing: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; text-size-adjust: 100%; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent; list-style-type: disc;">have not received two NP grades. Students who have received two NP grades shall be excluded from electing courses on a P/NP basis for one quarter and</li><li style="box-sizing: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; text-size-adjust: 100%; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent; list-style-type: disc; text-align: left;">are not repeating a course in which a grade of C-, D+, D, D- or F has been earned. Courses in which a letter grade is received may NOT be repeated on a P/NP&nbsp; basis. Courses originally taken on a P/NP&nbsp; basis may be repeated on the same basis or for a letter grade.</li></ul><p style="box-sizing: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; text-size-adjust: 100%; vertical-align: baseline; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; line-height: 1.6em; color: rgb(43, 43, 43); font-family: Lato, Helvetica, Arial, Lucida, sans-serif;">C) During Summer Sessions, for GE courses that are grading optional (letter grade OR P/NP), students are allowed to enroll in one grading option course (up to 5 units) under P/NP if they<br style="box-sizing: inherit;">are:</p><ul style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; text-size-adjust: 100%; vertical-align: baseline; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; line-height: 26px; color: rgb(43, 43, 43); font-family: Lato, Helvetica, Arial, Lucida, sans-serif;"><li style="box-sizing: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; text-size-adjust: 100%; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent; list-style-type: disc;">are in good academic standing (2.0 or higher term and cumulative GPA) and</li><li style="box-sizing: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; text-size-adjust: 100%; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent; list-style-type: disc;">have not received two NP grades. Students who have received two NP grades shall be excluded from electing courses on a P/NP basis for one quarter and</li><li style="box-sizing: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; text-size-adjust: 100%; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent; list-style-type: disc;">are not repeating a course in which a grade of C-, D+, D, D- or F has been earned.&nbsp; Courses in which a letter grade is received may NOT be repeated on a P/NP&nbsp; basis. Courses originally taken on a P/NP&nbsp; basis may be repeated on the same basis or for a letter grade.</li></ul><h5 style="box-sizing: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 10px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 13px; text-size-adjust: 100%; vertical-align: baseline; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; color: rgb(43, 43, 43); line-height: 1em; font-weight: 500; font-family: Lato, Helvetica, Arial, Lucida, sans-serif;">Passed/Not Passed and Equivalent Letter Grades</h5><p style="box-sizing: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; text-size-adjust: 100%; vertical-align: baseline; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; line-height: 1.6em; color: rgb(43, 43, 43); font-family: Lato, Helvetica, Arial, Lucida, sans-serif;">In order to receive a Passed “P” grade, you must achieve a grade of&nbsp;<span style="box-sizing: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; text-size-adjust: 100%; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent; font-weight: 700;">C or better.</span>&nbsp;Work done at the level of C- or below will be given a Not Passed “NP” and you will earn no units toward graduation.</p></p></blockquote>
</dd>
<p></p>
<dt class="show_hide" style="cursor: pointer; font-weight:normal;"><span class="toggle-plus">+</span> Repeating Courses: Do I have to repeat a course that I received a C- in?</dt>
<dd style="display:none">
<blockquote><p><p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;">Grades above an “F” do not have to be repeated (with the exception of the Ethics course requirements (ENGR 183EW, ENGR 185EW, BIOENGR&nbsp;165EW), English 3, Subject A, English as a Second Language, and American History and Institutions required courses which all must be passed with a minimum grade of “C”).</p><p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;">If a course is required for your major and you receive an “F”, you must repeat it.</p><p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;">You may have the option to repeat courses in which you have received a “C-” or lower grade or NP if you have not previously repeated that course.</p><p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;">Some Departments (such as Chem) recommend that students earn at least a “C-” or higher before going on to the next level course and this information is normally specified in the requisite information in the course description such as:<br>Chem 20B. Chemical Energetics and Change. (4)&nbsp;<a class="mce-item-anchor" style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; color: #1e4b87; background: transparent;" name="50655234_pgfId-1223988" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; color: #1e4b87; background: transparent;"></a>Lecture, three hours; discussion, one hour. Enforced requisites: course 20A or&nbsp;20AH, and Mathematics 31A,&nbsp;<strong style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;">with grades of C- or bette</strong>r.</p><p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;">Some departments (such as Math) may have credit limitations on repeats which are usually noted in the General catalog in the section for that department under Credit Limitations such as:<br>Credit Limitations:&nbsp;<strong style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;"><em style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;">For lower division mathematics courses</em></strong>, students may not take or repeat a course for credit if it is a requisite for a more advanced lower division course for which they already have credit. This applies in particular to the repetition of courses (e.g., if students wish to repeat Mathematics 31B, they must do so before completing course 32B; if students wish to repeat Mathematics 3B or 31B or 32A, they must do so before completing course 33A).</p><p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;">You must meet certain&nbsp;<a style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration: none; color: #1e4b87; background: transparent;" title="Degree Candidate Information" href="http://www.seasoasa.ucla.edu/degree-candidate-information/" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration: none; color: #1e4b87; background: transparent;" data-mce-href="http://www.seasoasa.ucla.edu/degree-candidate-information/">GPA requirements to graduate</a>. If you receive a grade lower than “C”, you are advised to meet with your OASA Counselor.</p><p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;">See more repeat rule information detailed below under “<a style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration: none; color: #1e4b87; background: transparent;" title="FAQs (Frequently Asked Questions)" href="http://www.seasoasa.ucla.edu/faqs-undergraduate-students/" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration: none; color: #1e4b87; background: transparent;" data-mce-href="http://www.seasoasa.ucla.edu/faqs-undergraduate-students/">How many courses can I repeat and will the first grade be removed from my transcrip</a>t? ”</p></p></blockquote>
</dd>
<p></p>
<dt class="show_hide" style="cursor: pointer; font-weight:normal;"><span class="toggle-plus">+</span> Repeating Courses: How many courses can I repeat and will the first grade be removed from my transcript?</dt>
<dd style="display:none">
<blockquote><p><p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;">The grade assigned each time you take a course will be permanently recorded on your transcript.</p><div style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; line-height: 23.8px; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; line-height: 23.8px; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;"><ol style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 23px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; list-style-position: inside; line-height: 26px; background: transparent;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 23px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; list-style-position: inside; line-height: 26px; background: transparent;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; list-style-position: outside; background: transparent;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; list-style-position: outside; background: transparent;">To improve the grade-point average, students may repeat only those courses in which they receive a grade of C- or lower; NP or U grades may be repeated to gain unit credit. Courses in which a letter grade is received may not be repeated on a P/NP or S/U basis. Courses originally taken on a P/NP or S/U basis may be repeated on the same basis or for a letter grade.</li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; list-style-position: outside; background: transparent;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; list-style-position: outside; background: transparent;">Repetition of a course more than once requires the approval of the College or school or the dean of the Graduate Division, and is granted only under extraordinary circumstances.</li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; list-style-position: outside; background: transparent;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; list-style-position: outside; background: transparent;">Degree credit for a course is given only once, but the grade assigned each time the course is taken is permanently recorded on the transcript.</li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; list-style-position: outside; background: transparent;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; list-style-position: outside; background: transparent;">For undergraduates who repeat a total of 16 units or less, only the most recently earned letter grades and grade<br>points are computed in the GPA. After repeating 16 units, however, the GPA is based on all letter grades assigned and total units attempted.</li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; list-style-position: outside; background: transparent;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; list-style-position: outside; background: transparent;">There is no guarantee that in a later term a course can be repeated (such as in cases when&nbsp; a course is deleted or no longer offered).&nbsp; In these cases a student should consult with their academic counselor to determine if there is an alternate course the student needs to take to satisfy a requirement.&nbsp; The alternate course would NOT count as a repeat of the original course.</li></ol></div></p></blockquote>
</dd>
<p></p>
<dt class="show_hide" style="cursor: pointer; font-weight:normal;"><span class="toggle-plus">+</span> What are the requirements for Dean's Honors?</dt>
<dd style="display:none">
<blockquote><p><span style="color: rgb(34, 34, 34); font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: small;">Students following the engineering curricula are eligible to be named to the Dean’s Honors List each term. Minimum requirements are a course load of at least 15 units (12 units of letter grade) with a grade-point average equal to or greater than 3.7. Students are not eligible for the Dean’s Honors List if they receive an Incomplete (I) or Not Passed (NP) grade or repeat a course. Only courses applicable to an undergraduate degree are considered toward eligibility for Dean’s Honors.</span><br data-mce-bogus="1"></p></blockquote>
</dd>
<p></dl>
<p><a name="enrollment-policy-deadline"></a></p>
<h3 style="border-bottom: 1px solid;">Enrollment Policies and Deadlines</h3>
<dl>
</p>
<dt class="show_hide" style="cursor: pointer; font-weight:normal;"><span class="toggle-plus">+</span> Appointment times for enrollment – how are they assigned?</dt>
<dd style="display:none">
<blockquote><p><p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;">Per the Registrar’s Office,<u style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;">&nbsp;U</u><u style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;">ndergraduates eligible to enroll for the next term do so during two randomly assigned appointments,<br>which fall within pass periods that are prioritized as follows:</u></p><p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;">Priority pass<br>160 or more degree units and declared candidacy to graduate in next two terms<br>160 or more units<br>New and re-entering students<br>135–159.9 units<br>90–134.9 units<br>45–89.9 units<br>0–44.9 units</p><p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;">The Registrar’s full explanation is detailed at the following website</p><pre>http://www.registrar.ucla.edu/Registration-Classes/Enrollment-Appointments/Enrollment-Appointments
</pre><p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;">Effective W16, in order to ensure that students have access to courses that are appropriate for their “true class” level,<br>a new system was devised by the UCLA campus that eliminated AP and IB units from the calculations of appointment times.<br>The new appointments are based on where a student is according to their true year in school, so that students may get access to the courses that they need in order to graduate.<br>For example, a true senior who needs a course for their major will no longer be competing for a course with a student who has senior<br>standing due to AP units.<br>Previously, the appointment times had more students at certain levels, creating large numbers of students enrolling&nbsp; in certain class size times (e.g., freshman, sophomores, juniors, seniors) that were not consistent with the actual class size.<br>In addition, some students would have an enrollment time that allowed them to take courses that they were not necessarily ready for academically.</p><p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;">The units from AP and IB tests still count and apply toward certain course degree requirements as detailed for UCLA Samueli School of Engineering at<br><a class="moz-txt-link-freetext" style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration: none; color: #1e4b87; background: transparent;" href="http://www.seasoasa.ucla.edu/curric-14-15/07ugrad-14.html" data-mce-href="http://www.seasoasa.ucla.edu/curric-14-15/07ugrad-14.html" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration: none; color: #1e4b87; background: transparent;">http://www.seasoasa.ucla.edu/curric-14-15/07ugrad-14.html</a><br>AP/IB units also will count towards class standing – for example, if a student wants to take a course that is restricted to<br>“JUNIORS AND ABOVE”&nbsp; a student can do so if the AP/IB units puts that student at the junior level.<br>The removal of AP/IB units only affects the system of assigning enrollment appointment times.<br>In addition, taking AP and IB courses counted toward a student’s admission to UCLA.</p><p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;">&nbsp;</p></p></blockquote>
</dd>

border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; height: 0px; line-height: 1; position: relative; bottom: 0.8em; background: transparent;">th</span></strong>&nbsp;Week at&nbsp;<strong style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;">5 PM</strong>.</li></ul></blockquote><p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;">For updated dates, please check this link:&nbsp;<a style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration: none; color: #1e4b87; background: transparent;" href="http://www.seasoasa.ucla.edu/deadlines-enrollment-policies/" data-mce-href="http://www.seasoasa.ucla.edu/deadlines-enrollment-policies/" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration: none; color: #1e4b87; background: transparent;">Drop Deadlines</a>.</p></p></blockquote>
</dd>
<p></p>
<dt class="show_hide" style="cursor: pointer; font-weight:normal;"><span class="toggle-plus">+</span> Dropping Courses: My friend, who is in the College of Letters & Science, says that I can drop a course through 10th week of the term. – Is that true?</dt>
<dd style="display:none">
<blockquote><p><span style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;" data-mce-style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;">No, the deadline (</span><a style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration: none; color: #1e4b87; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; line-height: 23.8px; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;" title="Deadlines &amp; Enrollment Policies" href="http://www.seasoasa.ucla.edu/deadlines-enrollment-policies/" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration: none; color: #1e4b87; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; line-height: 23.8px; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;" data-mce-href="http://www.seasoasa.ucla.edu/deadlines-enrollment-policies/">Deadlines and Enrollment Policies</a><span style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;" data-mce-style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;">) to drop a non-impacted course for UCLA Samueli School of Engineering students is Friday of fourth week of&nbsp;</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;" data-mce-style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;">the term via myUCLA until 5 p.m., even if it is an &nbsp;L&amp;S course. The deadline to drop an impacted course is second week of the term. The new&nbsp;</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;" data-mce-style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;">deadline to add any course is Friday of third week.</span></p></blockquote>
</dd>
<p></p>
<dt class="show_hide" style="cursor: pointer; font-weight:normal;"><span class="toggle-plus">+</span> Dropping vs. Withdrawing: What is the difference between dropping a course and withdrawing?</dt>
<dd style="display:none">
<blockquote><p><span style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;" data-mce-style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;">To “drop” a course means to dis-enroll from one (or more) specific course(s), while continuing to attend others. UCLA Samueli School of Engineering&nbsp;students must meet&nbsp;</span><a style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration: none; color: #1e4b87; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; line-height: 23.8px; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;" title="Deadlines &amp; Enrollment Policies" href="http://www.seasoasa.ucla.edu/deadlines-enrollment-policies/" data-mce-href="http://www.seasoasa.ucla.edu/deadlines-enrollment-policies/" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration: none; color: #1e4b87; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; line-height: 23.8px; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;">drop deadlines</a>&nbsp;<span style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;" data-mce-style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;">and must be enrolled in a minimum of 12 units per term. To “withdraw” means to discontinue attendance in ALL courses in which you are enrolled.&nbsp;UCLA Samueli School of Engineering&nbsp;students thinking of withdrawing<span style="color: #2b2b2b; font-family: Lato, Helvetica, Arial, Lucida, sans-serif;" data-mce-style="color: #2b2b2b; font-family: Lato, Helvetica, Arial, Lucida, sans-serif;">&nbsp;are encouraged to reach out to the&nbsp;</span><a href="https://www.seasoasa.ucla.edu/counselors/" target="_blank" rel="noopener" data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?q=https://www.seasoasa.ucla.edu/counselors/&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1611771272551000&amp;usg=AFQjCNH2lhlBJr3Bva5SGk55Cm5_3Nxs9A" style="box-sizing: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; text-size-adjust: 100%; vertical-align: baseline; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; color: #0d4481; font-family: Lato, Helvetica, Arial, Lucida, sans-serif;" data-mce-style="box-sizing: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; text-size-adjust: 100%; vertical-align: baseline; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; color: #0d4481; font-family: Lato, Helvetica, Arial, Lucida, sans-serif;">academic counselors&nbsp;</a><span style="color: #2b2b2b; font-family: Lato, Helvetica, Arial, Lucida, sans-serif;" data-mce-style="color: #2b2b2b; font-family: Lato, Helvetica, Arial, Lucida, sans-serif;">so that we can best advise them on their absence and help in their return</span>. Withdrawal requests can be submitted to the&nbsp;<a href="https://sa.ucla.edu/messagecenter/onestop/home/postmessage?topicid=242" data-mce-href="../../../messagecenter/onestop/home/postmessage?topicid=242">petitions queue</a> and are subject to review and approval by the Dean. You may file a request to withdraw for consideration only if you have not taken any final examinations or otherwise completed the work in any of your classes.</span></p></blockquote>
</dd>
<p></p>
<dt class="show_hide" style="cursor: pointer; font-weight:normal;"><span class="toggle-plus">+</span> Enrollment Options: Need help with enrollment options in undergraduate courses?</dt>
<dd style="display:none">
<blockquote><p><p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;">The following tips can be helpful when you are enrolling each term:</p><p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;">– prepare ahead by logging onto UCLA Samueli School of Engineering&nbsp;<a style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration: none; color: #1e4b87; background: transparent;" title="Degree Audit Reporting System (DARS)" href="http://www.seasoasa.ucla.edu/dars/" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration: none; color: #1e4b87; background: transparent;" data-mce-href="http://www.seasoasa.ucla.edu/dars/">Degree Audit Reporting System (DARS)</a>&nbsp;and knowing your course options needed to degree completion AND&nbsp;schedule an appointment to see your&nbsp;<a style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration: none; color: #1e4b87; background: transparent;" title="Counselors" href="http://www.seasoasa.ucla.edu/counselors/" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration: none; color: #1e4b87; background: transparent;" data-mce-href="http://www.seasoasa.ucla.edu/counselors/">Academic Counselor&nbsp;</a>BEFORE your enrollment begins</p><p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;">– do NOT enroll in time conflicted courses on the assumption that you will get into another section or a more preferred course at a later date</p><p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;">– when you begin to enroll, if you get a message from myUCLA stating the you do not meet the per-requisite or enrollment restrictions<a style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration: none; color: #1e4b87; background: transparent;" href="http://www.seasoasa.ucla.edu/faqs-undergraduate-students/" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration: none; color: #1e4b87; background: transparent;" data-mce-href="http://www.seasoasa.ucla.edu/faqs-undergraduate-students/">&nbsp;refer&nbsp;</a>to here<a style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration: none; color: #1e4b87; background: transparent;" title="Prerequisite - URSA says I do not meet the requisites, what is the problem? top of page" href="http://www.seasoasa.ucla.edu/faqs#pre-req" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration: none; color: #1e4b87; background: transparent;" data-mce-href="http://www.seasoasa.ucla.edu/faqs#pre-req">.</a><br data-mce-bogus="1"></p><p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;">–&nbsp;&nbsp; if you are attempting to enroll in a course and the course is closed,&nbsp; it is best&nbsp;that you&nbsp;EMAIL the lead counselor of the department that the course&nbsp;is under (e.g. CS course – email CS Counselor, Math course – email Math Counselor) BEFORE the term begins. Once the term&nbsp;starts&nbsp;there be limited assistance&nbsp;a counselor can give you, so&nbsp;be open to work with us.</p><p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;">The following contacts can update you as to&nbsp;the enrollment status of courses&nbsp;in their departments:</p><p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px;
