<p></p>
<dt class="show_hide" style="cursor: pointer; font-weight:normal;"><span class="toggle-plus">+</span> Enrollment Restriction: myUCLA will not let me enroll due to an enrollment restriction and the course is needed for my major – how can I get enrolled?</dt>
<dd style="display:none">
<blockquote><p><p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;">Many departments limit FIRST pass enrollment to students in that department’s major(s) and then open the course enrollment to other majors either: Specific to Chemistry –&nbsp;<a style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration: none; color: #1e4b87; background: transparent;" title="Chemistry Department" href="http://www.seasoasa.ucla.edu/faqs-undergraduate-students/#chemistry-department" data-mce-href="http://www.seasoasa.ucla.edu/faqs-undergraduate-students/#chemistry-department" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration: none; color: #1e4b87; background: transparent;">click here</a><br data-mce-bogus="1"></p><p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;">–&nbsp;during SECOND pass.&nbsp; This is the case with most UCLA Samueli School of Engineering courses (e.g. Bioengineering courses have a first pass enrollment restriction to bioengineering majors, then the courses open to other UCLA Samueli School of Engineering majors second pass).</p><p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;">OR</p><p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;">– specific to Com Sci 31, fall term offerings, after new student Summer Orientation (late August)</p><p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;">Priority Enrollment-&nbsp; myUCLA will not allow priority enrollment for courses that have a wait list option only.&nbsp; You must add yourself to the wait list during your FIRST pass.</p></p></blockquote>
</dd>
<p></p>
<dt class="show_hide" style="cursor: pointer; font-weight:normal;"><span class="toggle-plus">+</span> Fee Reduction: I heard I can enroll in 10 units or less and get my fees reduced. Is this true?</dt>
<dd style="display:none">
<blockquote><p><span style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;" data-mce-style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;">UCLA Samueli School of Engineering undergraduates must enroll in 12-21 units each quarter. Students wishing to enroll in less than 12 units or more than 21 units must obtain approval by petition to the Associate Dean, 6426 Boelter Hall, prior to enrollment. Filing a petition does not guarantee approval. Normally UCLA Samueli School of Engineering students are only approved, by petition, to enroll in less than 12 units for reasons of: final term before degree completion and only needs less than 12 units to complete degree, employment with verification that student is working 20 or more hours a week or due to on going medical limitations with verification from doctor or trained professional,&nbsp; Students approved by petition to enroll in 10 units or less&nbsp;may only be eligible for&nbsp;reduced fees as&nbsp;outlined at&nbsp;</span><a style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration: none; color: #1e4b87; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; line-height: 23.8px; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;" title="Degree Audit" href="http://www.seasoasa.ucla.edu/degree-candidate-information/" data-mce-href="http://www.seasoasa.ucla.edu/degree-candidate-information/" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration: none; color: #1e4b87; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; line-height: 23.8px; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;">fee reduction</a><span style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;" data-mce-style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;">. For more information go to the UCLA Samueli School of Engineering Office of Academic and Student Affairs, 6426BH.</span></p></blockquote>
</dd>
<p></p>

<dt class="show_hide" style="cursor: pointer; font-weight:normal;"><span class="toggle-plus">+</span> Graduate Courses: As an undergraduate can I enroll in a graduate level course (courses numbered 200 and above)?</dt>
<dd style="display:none">
<blockquote><p><span style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;" data-mce-style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;">UCLA Samueli School of Engineering undergraduate students are not allowed to enroll in graduate level courses without first obtaining approval by petition at 6426BH.</span><br style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;" data-mce-style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;"><span style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;" data-mce-style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;">See your UCLA Samueli School of Engineering Academic Counselor for more details. Students&nbsp; must meet requisites and have at minimum a 3.0 GPA for approval consideration.</span></p></blockquote>
</dd>

<dd style="display:none">
<blockquote><p><p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;">Based on class level, enrollment appointments are assigned randomly within the times and dates shown at the Registrar’s and are based on student status when appointments are assigned.&nbsp; Find exact enrollment appointment times through&nbsp;<a style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration: none; color: #1e4b87; background: transparent;" href="http://www.ursa.ucla.edu/" data-mce-href="http://www.ursa.ucla.edu/" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;">If you are a senior nearing graduation you are advised make sure you have declared a&nbsp;<a style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration: none; color: #1e4b87; background: transparent;" title="What is a degree expected term and when should I declare mine?" href="http://www.registrar.ucla.edu/soc/policy.htm#Anchor-Declaration-36621" data-mce-href="http://www.registrar.ucla.edu/soc/policy.htm#Anchor-Declaration-36621" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;" data-mce-style="color: #222222; margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px none; outline: currentcolor none 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; <dd style="display:none">
<blockquote><p><p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; You are advised&nbsp;to check your study list during the second week of each quarter to confirm your enrollment (checking second week will give you time to add or drop a course by the UCLA Samueli School of Engineering third week add deadline and fourth week drop deadline of non-impacted courses, if changes are needed). <h3 style="border-bottom: 1px solid;">Faculty Advising Questions</h3>
<dl>
</p>
<dt class="show_hide" style="cursor: pointer; font-weight:normal;"><span class="toggle-plus">+</span> Availability: How would I know when a faculty member is available to meet?</dt>
<dd style="display:none">
<blockquote><p><span style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;" data-mce-style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;">On&nbsp;</span><a style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration: none; color: #1e4b87; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; line-height: 23.8px; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;" href="http://my.engineering.ucla.edu/" data-mce-href="http://my.engineering.ucla.edu/" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration: none; color: #1e4b87; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; line-height: 23.8px; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;">MyEngineering</a><span style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;" data-mce-style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;">, the student can click on “Change/View Advisors” and they can see each professor’s advising hours and office location.&nbsp; They can also click “Contact” for the instructor’s email address.</span></p></blockquote>
</dd>
<p></p>
<dt class="show_hide" style="cursor: pointer; font-weight:normal;"><span class="toggle-plus">+</span> Completion: How would I know that my visit has been recorded?</dt>
<dd style="display:none">
<blockquote><p><span style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;" data-mce-style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;">Students who have not yet had a recorded meeting with a faculty member during the current school year will get a warning message when they log&nbsp;</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;" data-mce-style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;">in to&nbsp;</span><a style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration: none; color: #1e4b87; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; line-height: 23.8px; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;" href="http://my.engineering.ucla.edu/" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration: none; color: #1e4b87; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; line-height: 23.8px; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;" data-mce-href="http://my.engineering.ucla.edu/">MyEngineering</a><span style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;" data-mce-style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;">.</span></p></blockquote>
</dd>
<p></p>
<dt class="show_hide" style="cursor: pointer; font-weight:normal;"><span class="toggle-plus">+</span> Discussion Content: What are we supposed to talk about with our Faculty Advisor?</dt>
<dd style="display:none">
<blockquote><p><span style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;" data-mce-style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;">You can ask them questions about the field that they are involved in.&nbsp; You can discuss research opportunities, whether or not to pursue graduate school, companies in the field that have hired UCLA graduates in the past, or you can even discuss how the faculty member ended up as a&nbsp;</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;" data-mce-style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;">professor.</span></p></blockquote>
</dd>
<p></p>
<dt class="show_hide" style="cursor: pointer; font-weight:normal;"><span class="toggle-plus">+</span> Frequency: How often am I supposed to meet with my faculty advisor?</dt>
<dd style="display:none">
<blockquote><p><span style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;" data-mce-style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;">UCLA Samueli School of Engineering students are expected to meet with their advisor at least once a year.&nbsp; Your faculty advisor will post his/her office hours on&nbsp;</span><a style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration: none; color: #1e4b87; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; line-height: 23.8px; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;" href="http://my.engineering.ucla.edu/" data-mce-href="http://my.engineering.ucla.edu/" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration: none; color: #1e4b87; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; line-height: 23.8px; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;">MyEngineering</a><span style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;" data-mce-style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;">.&nbsp; Those students who have not met with their faculty advisor by the beginning of the 4th week of the spring quarter will have holds placed on their records.&nbsp; Students are strongly encouraged to meet with their faculty advisors during the faculty member’s special advising hours during 2nd or 3rd week, but they may also try to contact them and set up meetings for other times.</span></p></blockquote>
</dd>
<p></p>
<dt class="show_hide" style="cursor: pointer; font-weight:normal;"><span class="toggle-plus">+</span> Holds: How can I get rid of a hold on my record?</dt>
<dd style="display:none">
<blockquote><p><span style="color: rgb(34, 34, 34); box-sizing: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; line-height: 23.8px;">After completing your faculty advising meeting, make sure that the faculty advisor records the meeting in&nbsp;</span><a href="http://my.engineering.ucla.edu/" target="_blank" data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?q=http://my.engineering.ucla.edu/&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1594492841227000&amp;usg=AFQjCNEAvQlUrHsp_4-lIzOfsXlAYLAFlw" style="color: rgb(30, 75, 135); box-sizing: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; text-decoration-line: none; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; line-height: 23.8px;">MyEngineering</a><span style="color: rgb(34, 34, 34); box-sizing: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; line-height: 23.8px;">. Once the meeting is recorded complete the faculty advising survey. A link will appear on your MyEngineering. If you do not meet with a faculty advisor, then the hold will not be removed until after first pass in spring quarter.&nbsp;</span><br></p></blockquote>
</dd>
<p></p>
<dt class="show_hide" style="cursor: pointer; font-weight:normal;"><span class="toggle-plus">+</span> Purpose: Why do I have to meet with my Faculty Advisor every year?</dt>
<dd style="display:none">
<blockquote><p><span style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;" data-mce-style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;">UCLA Samueli School of Engineering feels that it is important for students to develop relationships with faculty.&nbsp; While students often don’t feel like they don’t have questions for the faculty early in their college careers, we feel that interacting with faculty early will make them feel more comfortable asking faculty for help in the future when it is more important.&nbsp; A letter of recommendation from your faculty advisor will be more meaningful if they have met with you multiple times throughout your career.</span></p></blockquote>
</dd>
<p></p>
<dt class="show_hide" style="cursor: pointer; font-weight:normal;"><span class="toggle-plus">+</span> Unavailable Advisor: What if my faculty advisor is unavailable or away on sabbatical?</dt>
<dd style="display:none">
<blockquote><p><span style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;" data-mce-style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;">Students can change faculty advisors on&nbsp;</span><a style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration: none; color: #1e4b87; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; line-height: 23.8px; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;" href="http://my.engineering.ucla.edu/" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration: none; color: #1e4b87; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; line-height: 23.8px; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;" data-mce-href="http://my.engineering.ucla.edu/">MyEngineering</a><span style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;" data-mce-style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;">&nbsp;by clicking on the “My Advisors” link.&nbsp; If the student does not want to change faculty advisors, they may see any faculty member in their department. The faculty has the ability to log in meetings with any student, even those who&nbsp;</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;" data-mce-style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;">are not their official assigned advisees.</span></p></blockquote>
</dd>
<p></p>
<dt class="show_hide" style="cursor: pointer; font-weight:normal;"><span class="toggle-plus">+</span> What is it: What is Faculty Advising and why am I supposed to do it?</dt>
<dd style="display:none">
<blockquote><p><span style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;" data-mce-style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;">Each UCLA Samueli School of Engineering student is assigned a faculty advisor within the student’s department.&nbsp; You can find out who your faculty advisor is by logging on to </span><a style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration: none; color: #1e4b87; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; line-height: 23.8px; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;" href="http://my.engineering.ucla.edu/" data-mce-href="http://my.engineering.ucla.edu/" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration: none; color: #1e4b87; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; line-height: 23.8px; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;">MyEngineering</a><span style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;" data-mce-style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;">.&nbsp; Faculty advisors are available if you have questions that your academic counselors may not be able to answer.&nbsp; They can provide advice about graduate school, undergraduate research, and job opportunities in the industry.&nbsp; It is our hope that you develop a relationship with them, especially since you may need them to write you a letter of recommendation.</span></p></blockquote>
</dd>
<p></dl>
<p><a name="graduation-issue"></a></p>
<h3 style="border-bottom: 1px solid;">Graduation Questions</h3>
<dl>
</p>
<dt class="show_hide" style="cursor: pointer; font-weight:normal;"><span class="toggle-plus">+</span> Degree Expected Term: What is a Degree Expected Term and when should I declare mine?</dt>
<dd style="display:none">
<blockquote><p><p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;">The Degree Expected Term is the year and quarter that a student plans to finish all his/her major requirements for completion of the bachelor’s degree.</p><p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;"><strong style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;">Deadline for declaration or change of bachelor’s degree candidacy on myUCLA – BEFORE 172 units for Engineering students</strong>.<br><a style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration: none; color: #1e4b87; background: transparent;" href="http://www.registrar.ucla.edu/Registration-Classes/Graduation/Declare-Candidacy" data-mce-href="http://www.registrar.ucla.edu/Registration-Classes/Graduation/Declare-Candidacy" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration: none; color: #1e4b87; background: transparent;">After 172 units there is a Registrar fee</a><br data-mce-bogus="1"></p></p></blockquote>
</dd>
<p></p>
<dt class="show_hide" style="cursor: pointer; font-weight:normal;"><span class="toggle-plus">+</span> Graduation Paperwork: I’m planning to graduate! What paperwork do I need to submit?</dt>
<dd style="display:none">
<blockquote><p><span style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;" data-mce-style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;">Students approaching graduation MUST follow the&nbsp;</span><a style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration: none; color: #1e4b87; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; line-height: 23.8px; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;" title="Degree Audit" href="http://www.seasoasa.ucla.edu/degree-candidate-information/" data-mce-href="http://www.seasoasa.ucla.edu/degree-candidate-information/" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration: none; color: #1e4b87; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; line-height: 23.8px; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;">degree audit process</a><span style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;" data-mce-style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;">&nbsp;in order for OASA to clarify exactly which requirements remain to be fulfilled for degree completion. This is a mandatory process students should be aware of at least two quarters prior to their degree expected term.</span></p></blockquote>
</dd>
<p></p>
<dt class="show_hide" style="cursor: pointer; font-weight:normal;"><span class="toggle-plus">+</span> Graduation Regalia: When and where do I purchase graduation regalia?</dt>

<dt class="show_hide" style="cursor: pointer; font-weight:normal;"><span class="toggle-plus">+</span> Catalog Year: What is my catalog year?</dt>
<dd style="display:none">
<blockquote><p><span style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;" data-mce-style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;">Your catalog year refers to the academic year you were admitted into your UCLA Samueli School of Engineering major. When referring to your curriculum requirements you should review what is outlined at&nbsp;</span><a style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;" data-mce-href="http://www.seasoasa.ucla.edu/curricular-requirements-department-information/">/undergraduates/curricular-requirements-department-information&nbsp;&nbsp;</a><span style="color: #222222; <dt class="show_hide" style="cursor: pointer; font-weight:normal;"><span class="toggle-plus">+</span> Degree Audit Recording System: What is DARS and where can I find out more about it?</dt>
<dd style="display:none">
<blockquote><p><span style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;" data-mce-style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;">DARS is the&nbsp;</span><a style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration: none; color: #1e4b87; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; line-height: 23.8px; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;" title="Degree Audit Reporting System (DARS)" href="http://www.seasoasa.ucla.edu/dars/" data-mce-href="http://www.seasoasa.ucla.edu/dars/" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration: none; color: #1e4b87; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; line-height: 23.8px; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;">Degree Audit Reporting System (DARS)</a><span style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;" data-mce-style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;">&nbsp;and you can find more information in that link.</span></p></blockquote>
</dd>
<p></p>
<dt class="show_hide" style="cursor: pointer; font-weight:normal;"><span class="toggle-plus">+</span> Double Major or Minor: Is it possible to double major or earn a minor?</dt>
<dd style="display:none">
<blockquote><p><p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;">HSSEAS students in good academic standing may be permitted a double major or minor. The second major must be outside HSSEAS (e.g. Electrical Engineering major and Economics major).&nbsp; HSSEAS students are not permitted to double major with two HSSEAS majors (e.g. Chemical Engineering and Civil Engineering).</p><p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;">To begin the possible option of adding a major or minor,</p><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 23px 16px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 26px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 23px 16px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 26px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;"><li style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;">investigate possible options – For a full list of MAJORS and&nbsp;MINORS offered at UCLA refer to the UCLA General Catalog<br><a style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration: none; color: #1e4b87; background: transparent;" href="http://catalog.registrar.ucla.edu/" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration: none; color: #1e4b87; background: transparent;" data-mce-href="http://catalog.registrar.ucla.edu/">http://catalog.registrar.ucla.edu/</a></li><li style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;">File an&nbsp;<strong style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;">Undergraduate Request to Double Major or Add Minor form</strong>&nbsp;at the Office of Academic and Student Affairs (OASA), 6426 BH.&nbsp; This form will start a review process by HSSEAS.</li><li style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;">HSSEAS also advises that students meet with the Department Counselors of the major or minor student is considering adding in order to understand those requirements.</li><li style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;">If HSSEAS determines that student meets HSSEAS eligibility for&nbsp;adding major or minor,&nbsp; student will be advised to complete a Change of Major petition which must be approved by the&nbsp;Department of the major or minor student is requesting to add and then returned to 6426 Boelter Hall for final processing. UCLA Samueli School of Engineering&nbsp;determines final approval of a double major or minor request – review is done on a case by case basis, filing the request does NOT guarantee approval.</li><li style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;"><span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: small;">PLEASE NOTE: No more than 20 upper-division units may be shared by both majors.</span><br data-mce-bogus="1"></li></ul><p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;">If you are interested in a double major or minor you should meet with your OASA Counselor at 6426 BH.</p></p></blockquote>
</dd>
<p></p>
<dt class="show_hide" style="cursor: pointer; font-weight:normal;"><span class="toggle-plus">+</span> Research Credit: I’m doing research with a professor/employer.  How do I get course credit for that?</dt>
<dd style="display:none">
<blockquote><p><p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;">There are a couple of courses you can take which will give you credit:&nbsp;<a style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration: none; color: #1e4b87; background: transparent;" href="http://www.seasoasa.ucla.edu/enrollment-in-courses" data-mce-href="http://www.seasoasa.ucla.edu/enrollment-in-courses" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration: none; color: #1e4b87; background: transparent;">95, 194, 195, 199</a>. More information can be found at that link.</p><p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;">Lower division research is&nbsp;<a style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration: none; color: #1e4b87; background: transparent;" href="http://www.ugresearchsci.ucla.edu/srpintro.htm" data-mce-href="http://www.ugresearchsci.ucla.edu/srpintro.htm" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration: none; color: #1e4b87; background: transparent;">SRP 99&nbsp;</a>and information can be found at that link.</p><p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;">For UCLA Samueli School of Engineering students, 99 contract forms must be submitted week 1 of the Fall, Winter, Spring term, to 6426BH, for review and approval. &nbsp;After UCLA Samueli School of Engineering approval, SRP add deadline, to submit contract form to SRP Office, is Friday at 5pm, second week of Fall, Winter, Spring term.&nbsp; For summer, contracts for all sessions are due to the SRP Office the Friday of 2<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; height: 0px; line-height: 1; position: relative; bottom: 0.8em; background: transparent;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; height: 0px; line-height: 1; position: relative; bottom: 0.8em; background: transparent;">nd</span>&nbsp;week during Session A/6 week.</p></p></blockquote>
</dd>
<p></p>
<dt class="show_hide" style="cursor: pointer; font-weight:normal;"><span class="toggle-plus">+</span> Technical Breadth Requirement: What is the Technical Breadth Requirement (TBR)?</dt>
<dd style="display:none">
<blockquote><p><p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;">Students following the 2006 or later catalog years, are required the technical breadth requirement.</p><p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;"><a style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration: none; color: #1e4b87; background: transparent;" title="Technical Breadth Area (TBA)" href="http://www.seasoasa.ucla.edu/undergraduate-technical-breadth-area-tba" data-mce-href="http://www.seasoasa.ucla.edu/undergraduate-technical-breadth-area-tba" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration: none; color: #1e4b87; background: transparent;">Technical Breadth Area (TBA)<strong style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;"><br></strong></a><br data-mce-bogus="1"></p><p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;">Students must declare their area using&nbsp;<a style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration: none; color: #1e4b87; background: transparent;" href="http://my.engineering.ucla.edu/" data-mce-href="http://my.engineering.ucla.edu/" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration: none; color: #1e4b87; background: transparent;">MyEngineering</a><br data-mce-bogus="1"></p><p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;">Instructions for declaring your technical breadth area on&nbsp;<a style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration: none; color: #1e4b87; background: transparent;" href="http://my.engineering.ucla.edu/" data-mce-href="http://my.engineering.ucla.edu/" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration: none; color: #1e4b87; background: transparent;">MyEngineering</a>&nbsp;are as<br>follows:</p><p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 23.8px; color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; At [<a style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration: none; color: #1e4b87; background: transparent;" href="http://my.engineering.ucla.edu/" data-mce-href="http://my.engineering.ucla.edu/" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration: none; color: #1e4b87; background: transparent;">MyEngineering</a>], in “My Profile” box, click on “About Me”<br>3. Locate “Technical Breadth Area” in the “View/Edit Profile Information”<br>box and select your TBA.</p></p></blockquote>
</dd>
<p></p>
<dt class="show_hide" style="cursor: pointer; font-weight:normal;"><span class="toggle-plus">+</span> Undeclared Engineering: I am an Undeclared Engineering major. How and when do I declare my major?</dt>
<dd style="display:none">
<blockquote><p><p>&nbsp;<br></p><p style="box-sizing: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; text-size-adjust: 100%; vertical-align: baseline; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; line-height: 1.6em; color: #2b2b2b; font-family: Lato, Helvetica, Arial, Lucida, sans-serif;" data-mce-style="box-sizing: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 1em; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; text-size-adjust: 100%; vertical-align: baseline; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; line-height: 1.6em; color: #2b2b2b; font-family: Lato, Helvetica, Arial, Lucida, sans-serif;">Being an Undeclared Engineering student means you are guaranteed the Engineering major of your choice if you meet the following criteria:</p><ol style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 23px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; text-size-adjust: 100%; vertical-align: baseline; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; list-style-position: inside; list-style-image: initial; line-height: 26px; color: #2b2b2b; font-family: Lato, Helvetica, Arial, Lucida, sans-serif;" data-mce-style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 23px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; text-size-adjust: 100%; vertical-align: baseline; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; list-style-position: inside; list-style-image: initial; line-height: 26px; color: #2b2b2b; font-family: Lato, Helvetica, Arial, Lucida, sans-serif;"><li style="box-sizing: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; text-size-adjust: 100%; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;" data-mce-style="box-sizing: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; text-size-adjust: 100%; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;">Declare your major between the beginning of Spring quarter of your freshman year and the beginning of Fall quarter of your sophomore year.</li><li style="box-sizing: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; text-size-adjust: 100%; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;" data-mce-style="box-sizing: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; text-size-adjust: 100%; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;">Have a minimum 2.700 GPA in Engineering preparatory courses at the time you declare.</li><li style="box-sizing: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; text-size-adjust: 100%; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;" data-mce-style="box-sizing: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; text-size-adjust: 100%; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;">Receive grades of C or better in all required major prep courses for the major in which you are interested.</li><li style="box-sizing: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; text-size-adjust: 100%; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;" data-mce-style="box-sizing: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; text-size-adjust: 100%; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;">Take and pass an introductory engineering course from the major you are mostly likely to choose, or take and pass an Engineering 96 Freshman Seminar – Introduction to Engineering Design.</li></ol><p style="box-sizing: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; text-size-adjust: 100%; vertical-align: baseline; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; line-height: 1.6em; color: #2b2b2b; font-family: Lato, Helvetica, Arial, Lucida, sans-serif;" data-mce-style="box-sizing: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; text-size-adjust: 100%; vertical-align: baseline; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; line-height: 1.6em; color: #2b2b2b; font-family: Lato, Helvetica, Arial, Lucida, sans-serif;">Students applying to Computer Science or Computer Science and Engineering must also complete COM SCI 31 with a C or better (not a C-) on the first attempt AND COM SCI 32 and 33 with a B- grades or better on the first attempt. Students applying to Computer Engineering must complete COM SCI 31 and EC ENGR 3 with a grade of C or better on the first attempt AND COM SCI 32 and EC ENGR M16/COM SCI M51A with a B- or better on the first attempt.<br style="box-sizing: inherit;" data-mce-style="box-sizing: inherit;">This guarantee only applies toward the first major change. Any subsequent major changes are not guaranteed; therefore make sure you are applying for a major in which you are genuinely interested.</p><p><span style="background-color: transparent; font-family: Arial; font-size: 11pt; white-space: pre-wrap; color: #222222;" data-mce-style="background-color: transparent; font-family: Arial; font-size: 11pt; white-space: pre-wrap; color: #222222;">Follow the Change of Major process detailed&nbsp; at&nbsp;https://www.seasoasa.ucla.edu/change-of-major/</span><br></p></p></blockquote>
</dd>
<p></p>
<dt class="show_hide" style="cursor: pointer; font-weight:normal;"><span class="toggle-plus">+</span> Writing Requirement - what is UCLA Samueli School of Engineering writing requirement?</dt>
<dd style="display:none">
<blockquote><p><p>(a) English Composition 3, which must be completed with a minimum grade of C by the end of the second year of enrollment at UCLA(this requirement may be satisfied by a score of 4 or 5 on the English Language and Composition or English Literature and Composition AP Exam);</p>
<p>(b) Engineering Writing; one 4-unit engineering ethics course chosen from BIOENGR 165EW, ENGR 181EW, 182EW 183EW or 185EW which must be completed with a minimum grade of C which also satisifes UCLA Samueli School of Engineering Ethics Requirement. <br></p>
<p><br></p></p></blockquote>
</dd>

<p><a name="student-opportunity"></a></p>
<h3 style="border-bottom: 1px solid;">Opportunities - MentorSEAS, Scholarships, Student Organizations</h3>
<dl>
</p>
<dt class="show_hide" style="cursor: pointer; font-weight:normal;"><span class="toggle-plus">+</span> MentorSEAS: What is the UCLA Engineering Mentorship Program (MentorSEAS)?</dt>
<dd style="display:none">
<blockquote><p><span style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;" data-mce-style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;">MentorSEAS is&nbsp;the official UCLA Engineering school-wide mentorship program designed to provide guidance, support, and networking of social, professional, and academic relationships to first year freshmen and transfer students in the School. Mentors (continuing engineering students) serve as role models by providing advice, being a good support system, and to assist with the transition to UCLA. Please visit the official&nbsp;</span><a style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration: none; color: #1e4b87; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; line-height: 23.8px; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;" href="http://mentorship.seas.ucla.edu/" data-mce-href="http://mentorship.seas.ucla.edu/" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration: none; color: #1e4b87; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; line-height: 23.8px; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;">MentorSEAS</a><span style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;" data-mce-style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;">&nbsp;site for more information about this great resource.</span></p></blockquote>
</dd>
<p></p>
<dt class="show_hide" style="cursor: pointer; font-weight:normal;"><span class="toggle-plus">+</span> Organizations: I want to announce an event to students, how can I do so?</dt>
<dd style="display:none">
<blockquote><p><h4 style="margin: 0in 0in 0.0001pt; font-size: 12pt; font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; color: #222222; line-height: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;" data-mce-style="margin: 0in 0in 0.0001pt; font-size: 12pt; font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; color: #222222; line-height: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;"><span style="font-size: 11.5pt; font-family: Helvetica, sans-serif; border: 1pt none windowtext; padding: 0in;" data-mce-style="font-size: 11.5pt; font-family: Helvetica, sans-serif; border: 1pt none windowtext; padding: 0in;">Samueli Engineering Office of Academic and Student Affairs (OASA) Policy and Procedure on Requests to Post Announcements, or Mass Email Students, Concerning Opportunities and Campus Events</span></h4><p style="color: #222222; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: small; font-weight: 400; margin: 0in 0in 0.0001pt; vertical-align: baseline; box-sizing: inherit; outline: 0px; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;" data-mce-style="color: #222222; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: small; font-weight: 400; margin: 0in 0in 0.0001pt; vertical-align: baseline; box-sizing: inherit; outline: 0px; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><span style="font-size: 10.5pt; font-family: Helvetica, sans-serif;" data-mce-style="font-size: 10.5pt; font-family: Helvetica, sans-serif;">Central School units such as the Office of Academic and Student Affairs and SEASnet&nbsp; are normally unable to comply with requests from groups to send mass emails to&nbsp;<span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: small;">Samueli Engineering&nbsp;</span>students. We do however realize that it is important for organizations to get their messages out to our students; therefore, we encourage the following options. If you are:<br><br></span></p><p style="color: #222222; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: small; font-weight: 400; margin: 0in 0in 0.0001pt; vertical-align: baseline; box-sizing: inherit; outline: 0px; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;" data-mce-style="color: #222222; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: small; font-weight: 400; margin: 0in 0in 0.0001pt; vertical-align: baseline; box-sizing: inherit; outline: 0px; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><strong><u><span style="font-size: 10.5pt; font-family: Helvetica, sans-serif; background: #eeeeee;" data-mce-style="font-size: 10.5pt; font-family: Helvetica, sans-serif; background: #eeeeee;">(a)&nbsp;&nbsp;<em><span style="border: 1pt none windowtext; padding: 0in;" data-mce-style="border: 1pt none windowtext; padding: 0in;">Samueli Engineering Student Organization&nbsp;</span></em>Please refer to the following communication tools:</span></u></strong></p><p style="color: #222222; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: small; font-weight: 400; margin: 0in 0in 0.0001pt; vertical-align: baseline; box-sizing: inherit; outline: 0px; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;" data-mce-style="color: #222222; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: small; font-weight: 400; margin: 0in 0in 0.0001pt; vertical-align: baseline; box-sizing: inherit; outline: 0px; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><span style="font-size: 11.5pt; font-family: Helvetica, sans-serif;" data-mce-style="font-size: 11.5pt; font-family: Helvetica, sans-serif;"><a style="color: #1155cc;" href="https://www.seasnet.ucla.edu/student-groups-communication-tools/" target="_blank" data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?q=https://www.seasnet.ucla.edu/student-groups-communication-tools/&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1597257899457000&amp;usg=AFQjCNHdFSreN_470zcnvz8-eubwtm4Rdg" data-mce-href="https://www.seasnet.ucla.edu/student-groups-communication-tools/" data-mce-style="color: #1155cc;">https://www.seasnet.ucla.edu/<wbr>student-groups-communication-<wbr>tools/<br><br></a></span></p><p style="color: #222222; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: small; font-weight: 400; margin: 0in 0in 0.0001pt; vertical-align: baseline;" data-mce-style="color: #222222; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: small; font-weight: 400; margin: 0in 0in 0.0001pt; vertical-align: baseline;"><span style="font-size: 10.5pt; font-family: Helvetica, sans-serif;" data-mce-style="font-size: 10.5pt; font-family: Helvetica, sans-serif;">(b)&nbsp;<em><span style="border: 1pt none windowtext; padding: 0in;" data-mce-style="border: 1pt none windowtext; padding: 0in;">School of Engineering Academic Departments</span></em>&nbsp;or a Group wanting to send a notice to<br>students in a particular&nbsp;<span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: small;">Samueli Engineering</span>&nbsp;department:<br>Each department MSO can authorize staff that they would like to have access to&nbsp;<a style="color: #1155cc;" href="http://my.engineering.ucla.edu/" target="_blank" data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?q=http://my.engineering.ucla.edu/&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1597257899457000&amp;usg=AFQjCNEYu-Z_16RqgnYTPVpmM9AKL_dNsA" data-mce-href="http://my.engineering.ucla.edu/" data-mce-style="color: #1155cc;"><span style="color: windowtext; border: 1pt none windowtext; padding: 0in;" data-mce-style="color: windowtext; border: 1pt none windowtext; padding: 0in;">MyEngineering</span></a>, which would allow the department to email students within their department.&nbsp;Sending announcements is up to the discretion of each department.&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: small;">Samueli Engineering</span>&nbsp;departments who wish to send a notice to all&nbsp;<span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: small;">Samueli Engineering</span>&nbsp;students can request a posting on SEASnet’s MOTD and the LCD panels.<br><br></span></p><p style="color: #222222; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: small; font-weight: 400; margin: 0in 0in 0.0001pt; vertical-align: baseline; box-sizing: inherit; outline: 0px; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;" data-mce-style="color: #222222; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: small; font-weight: 400; margin: 0in 0in 0.0001pt; vertical-align: baseline; box-sizing: inherit; outline: 0px; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><span style="font-size: 10.5pt; font-family: Helvetica, sans-serif;" data-mce-style="font-size: 10.5pt; font-family: Helvetica, sans-serif;">(c)<em><u><span style="border: 1pt none windowtext; padding: 0in;" data-mce-style="border: 1pt none windowtext; padding: 0in;">&nbsp;Industrial Affiliates or Other Company Employers</span></u></em><br>In an attempt to disseminate all internship/job opportunities and advertise all on campus industry recruitment events, we have created the</span></p><p style="color: #222222; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: small; font-weight: 400; margin: 0in 0in 0.0001pt; vertical-align: baseline; box-sizing: inherit; outline: 0px; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;" data-mce-style="color: #222222; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: small; font-weight: 400; margin: 0in 0in 0.0001pt; vertical-align: baseline; box-sizing: inherit; outline: 0px; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><span style="font-size: 10.5pt; font-family: Helvetica, sans-serif;" data-mce-style="font-size: 10.5pt; font-family: Helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: small;">Samueli Engineering</span>&nbsp;Internship/Job Clearinghouse website.</span></p><p style="color: #222222; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: small; font-weight: 400; margin: 0in 0in 0.0001pt; vertical-align: baseline; box-sizing: inherit; outline: 0px; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;" data-mce-style="color: #222222; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: small; font-weight: 400; margin: 0in 0in 0.0001pt; vertical-align: baseline; box-sizing: inherit; outline: 0px; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><span style="font-size: 10.5pt; font-family: Helvetica, sans-serif;" data-mce-style="font-size: 10.5pt; font-family: Helvetica, sans-serif;">Anyone interested in posting an internship/job opportunity on this webpage should e-mail&nbsp;<span style="border: 1pt none windowtext; padding: 0in;" data-mce-style="border: 1pt none windowtext; padding: 0in;"><a style="color: #1155cc;" href="mailto:jobsinternships@seas.ucla.edu" target="_blank" data-mce-href="mailto:jobsinternships@seas.ucla.edu" data-mce-style="color: #1155cc;"><span style="color: windowtext;" data-mce-style="color: windowtext;">jobsinternships@seas.<wbr>ucla.edu</span></a></span>. All Industrial Affiliates and other company employers are also encouraged to post their current job/internship opportunities on UCLA Handshake through the Career Center.<br><br>Additional information on the UCLA Samueli Undergraduate Internship Program can be found at&nbsp;<a style="color: #1155cc;" href="https://www.seasoasa.ucla.edu/undergraduate-internship-program/" target="_blank" data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?q=https://www.seasoasa.ucla.edu/undergraduate-internship-program/&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1597257899457000&amp;usg=AFQjCNFrdvu7eK6z7_fZ13x5NLN_5zx2VA" data-mce-href="https://www.seasoasa.ucla.edu/undergraduate-internship-program/" data-mce-style="color: #1155cc;"><span style="color: windowtext; border: 1pt none windowtext; padding: 0in;" data-mce-style="color: windowtext; border: 1pt none windowtext; padding: 0in;">https://www.seasoasa.ucla.<wbr>edu/undergraduate-internship-<wbr>program/</span></a></span></p><p style="color: #222222; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: small; font-weight: 400; margin: 0in 0in 0.0001pt; vertical-align: baseline; box-sizing: inherit; outline: 0px; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;" data-mce-style="color: #222222; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: small; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><span style="font-size: 10.5pt; font-family: Helvetica, sans-serif;" data-mce-style="font-size: 10.5pt; font-family: Helvetica, sans-serif;"><br>Industrial Affiliates or Other Company Employers may also want to work directly with the&nbsp;<span style="color: windowtext; border: 1pt none windowtext; padding: 0in;" data-mce-style="color: windowtext; border: 1pt none windowtext; padding: 0in;"><u><span style="color: rgb(34, 34, 34); font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: small;">Samueli Engineering&nbsp;</span></u><a style="color: #1155cc;" href="https://samueli.ucla.edu/student-clubs-organizations" target="_blank" data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?q=https://samueli.ucla.edu/student-clubs-organizations&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1597257899457000&amp;usg=AFQjCNExq__zHXr4fuqP3I11wi-TuSfXVA" data-mce-href="https://samueli.ucla.edu/student-clubs-organizations" data-mce-style="color: #1155cc;"><u>stud</u>ent organizations&nbsp;</a></span>who can assist with scheduling on-campus recruitment events.<br><br></span></p><p style="color: #222222; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: small; font-weight: 400; margin: 0in 0in 0.0001pt; vertical-align: baseline; box-sizing: inherit; outline: 0px; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;" data-mce-style="color: #222222; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: small;
