background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><span style="font-size: 10.5pt; font-family: Helvetica, sans-serif;" data-mce-style="font-size: 10.5pt; font-family: Helvetica, sans-serif;">(d)&nbsp;<em><u><span style="border: 1pt none windowtext; padding: 0in;" data-mce-style="border: 1pt none windowtext; padding: 0in;">UCLA Offices and Student Groups Outside of the School of Engineering (HSSEAS)&nbsp;</span></u></em></span></p><p style="color: #222222; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: small; font-weight: 400; margin: 0in 0in 0.0001pt; vertical-align: baseline; box-sizing: inherit; outline: 0px; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;" data-mce-style="color: #222222; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: small; font-weight: 400; margin: 0in 0in 0.0001pt; vertical-align: baseline; box-sizing: inherit; outline: 0px; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><span style="font-size: 10.5pt; font-family: Helvetica, sans-serif;" data-mce-style="font-size: 10.5pt; font-family: Helvetica, sans-serif;">may want to submit a Registrar’s Service Request (RSR)&nbsp;<a style="color: #1155cc;" href="https://saweb.uclanet.ucla.edu/SAWeb/ServiceRequest/Rsr/ManageRequest.aspx" target="_blank" data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?q=https://saweb.uclanet.ucla.edu/SAWeb/ServiceRequest/Rsr/ManageRequest.aspx&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1597257899457000&amp;usg=AFQjCNHDwdYm3hdxk_XdMvPSFNReYTXu_w" data-mce-href="https://saweb.uclanet.ucla.edu/SAWeb/ServiceRequest/Rsr/ManageRequest.aspx" data-mce-style="color: #1155cc;"><span style="color: windowtext; border: 1pt none windowtext; padding: 0in;" data-mce-style="color: windowtext; border: 1pt none windowtext; padding: 0in;">The Registrar’s Service Request</span></a>&nbsp;(RSR) application is used by staff, faculty, and student organizations to submit requests for student data. Services do include mass e-mails to students.</span></p><h4><br></h4></p></blockquote>
</dd>
<p></p>
<dt class="show_hide" style="cursor: pointer; font-weight:normal;"><span class="toggle-plus">+</span> Scholarships: Where can I find information regarding scholarships?</dt>
<dd style="display:none">
<blockquote><p><span style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;" data-mce-style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;">For current scholarship information for undergraduate UCLA Samueli School of Engineering students, as well as links to other sources on campus, go to&nbsp;</span><a style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration: none; color: #1e4b87; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; line-height: 23.8px; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;" href="http://www.seasoasa.ucla.edu/scholarships-for-undergraduates/" data-mce-href="http://www.seasoasa.ucla.edu/scholarships-for-undergraduates/" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration: none; color: #1e4b87; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; line-height: 23.8px; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;">Scholarships.</a></p></blockquote>
</dd>
<p></p>
<dt class="show_hide" style="cursor: pointer; font-weight:normal;"><span class="toggle-plus">+</span> Student Organizations in Samueli Engineering: where can I find a list?</dt>
<dd style="display:none">
<blockquote><p><p>Information about&nbsp;<span style="color: rgb(34, 34, 34); font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: small;">Samueli Engineering</span>&nbsp;Student Organizations can be found at</p><a href="http://engineering.ucla.edu/student-clubs/" data-mce-href="http://engineering.ucla.edu/student-clubs/">http://engineering.ucla.edu/student-clubs/</a></p></blockquote>
</dd>
<p></dl>
<p><a name="transfer-course"></a></p>
<h3 style="border-bottom: 1px solid;">Transferring Courses</h3>
<dl>
</p>
<dt class="show_hide" style="cursor: pointer; font-weight:normal;"><span class="toggle-plus">+</span> Another University Course Credit: What do I do if I want to take courses at another school during the summer?</dt>
<dd style="display:none">
<blockquote><p>Community College/Lower Division Transfer Limit.&nbsp; After completing 105 quarter units toward the degree in all institutions attended, students are allowed no further unit credit for courses completed at a community college or for lower division courses completed at any institution outside of the University of California.</p></blockquote>
</dd>
<p></p>
<dt class="show_hide" style="cursor: pointer; font-weight:normal;"><span class="toggle-plus">+</span> Transfer Credit: My transfer credits on my DPR aren’t matching what my counselor told me.  What’s wrong?</dt>
<dd style="display:none">
<blockquote><p><h4 style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 10px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 18px; vertical-align: baseline; color: #333333; line-height: 1em; font-weight: 500; font-family: Lato, Helvetica, Arial, Lucida, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 10px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 18px; vertical-align: baseline; color: #333333; line-height: 1em; font-weight: 500; font-family: Lato, Helvetica, Arial, Lucida, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;"><span style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;" data-mce-style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;">The DPR was designed for students in the College of Letters &amp; Science and shows the Admissions Office’s evaluation of your transfer credit, NOT the UCLA Samueli School of Engineering evaluation.&nbsp; The UCLA Samueli School of Engineering evaluation normally gives more usable credit, because it reflects your major requirements, which the DPR&nbsp;</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;" data-mce-style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;">does not. To verify what credit you have&nbsp;see a Counselor, 6426BH.</span><br></h4></p></blockquote>
</dd>
<p></p>
<dt class="show_hide" style="cursor: pointer; font-weight:normal;"><span class="toggle-plus">+</span> UCLA Extension: Can I take courses through UCLA extension to fill in classes while I’m at UCLA Samueli School of Engineering?</dt>
<dd style="display:none">
<blockquote><p><span style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;" data-mce-style="color: #222222; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 23.8px;">The Henry Samueli School of Engineering and Applied Science (UCLA Samueli School of Engineering) does not permit continuing UCLA Samueli School of Engineering students to enroll in courses toward degree completion through UCLA Extension’s Concurrent Enrollment program. There are no exceptions to this policy – please refer to&nbsp;</span><a style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration: none; color: #1e4b87; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; line-height: 23.8px; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;" href="http://www.seasoasa.ucla.edu/concurrent-enrollment-thru-ucla-extension" data-mce-style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration: none; color: #1e4b87; font-family: ProximaNova, Verdana, sans-serif; line-height: 23.8px; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;" data-mce-href="http://www.seasoasa.ucla.edu/concurrent-enrollment-thru-ucla-extension">http://www.seasoasa.ucla.edu/concurrent-enrollment-thru-ucla-extension</a></p></blockquote>
</dd>
<p></dl>
